## Gives count, mean, standard deviation, standard error 
of the mean, and confidence interval (default 95%).
##   data: a data frame.
##   measurevar: the name of a column that contains the 
variable to be summariezed
##   groupvars: a vector containing names of columns 
that contain grouping variables
##   na.rm: a boolean that indicates whether to ignore 
NA's
##   conf.interval: the percent range of the confidence 
interval (default is 95%)
##
##  Modified from:  http://www.cookbook-
r.com/Graphs/Plotting_means_and_error_bars_(ggplot2)/
##  Retrieved:      14/03/2016
summarySE <- function(data=NULL, measurevar, 
groupvars=NULL, na.rm=FALSE,
                      conf.interval=.95, .drop=TRUE) {
  library(plyr)
  
  # New version of length which can handle NA's: if 
na.rm==T, don't count them
  length2 <- function (x, na.rm=FALSE) {
    if (na.rm) sum(!is.na(x))
    else       length(x)
  }
  
  # This does the summary. For each group's data frame, 
return a vector with
  # N, mean, and sd
  datac <- ddply(data, groupvars, .drop=.drop,
                 .fun = function(xx, col) {
                   c(N = length2(xx[[col]], 
na.rm=na.rm),
                     median = median(xx[[col]], 
na.rm=na.rm),
                     mean = mean(xx[[col]], 
na.rm=na.rm),
                     sd   = sd(xx[[col]], na.rm=na.rm),
                     q25 = 
as.numeric(quantile(xx[[col]],0.25,na.rm=na.rm)),
                     q75 = 
as.numeric(quantile(xx[[col]],0.75,na.rm=na.rm)) 
                   )
                 },
==PAGE:105==
                 measurevar
  )
  
  # Rename the "mean" column    
  datac <- rename(datac, c("mean" = measurevar))
  
  datac$se <- datac$sd / sqrt(datac$N)  # Calculate 
standard error of the mean
  
  # Confidence interval multiplier for standard error
  # Calculate t-statistic for confidence interval: 
  # e.g., if conf.interval is .95, use .975 
(above/below), and use df=N-1
  ciMult <- qt(conf.interval/2 + .5, datac$N-1)
  datac$ci <- datac$se * ciMult
  
  return(datac)
}
==PAGE:106==
## Divides a dataframe based on output from CellProfiler into bins.
##  Must contain global position scale named: Globalposition_X
##
## Template: CollectInBins(mydata,n)
##
## Input:
##    mydata:  Data frame with output from
##         n:  Number of partitions each image is to be devided into. 
##
## Output:
##      Single object, list of variables containing:
##            mean of all features. One mean for each bin.
##            Xbin: A vector linking the observations in the
##                  original data "mydata" to the binned output.
CollectInBins <- function(mydata,n){
  #n is number of bins each image should be divided into
  
  # Divide dataset with sliding window
  nbins <- 18*n # number of bins
  overl <- 0 # percentage overlap
  ran <-  range(mydata$Globalposition_X)
  bin.size <- (ran[2]-ran[1])/nbins
  
  # Create starting point for each bin and endpoint of last
  win <- cumsum(matrix(bin.size*(1-overl), ncol = (nbins-1)/(1-
overl)+1))+ran[1]+bin.size*overl
  
  # Allocate a position bin to each sample
  mydata$Xbin <- as.factor(findInterval(mydata$Globalposition_X,win))
  
  # Aggregate data into Xbins separated by class
  mydata.aggregate <- aggregate(mydata[,10:136],list(mydata$Xbin,mydata$Class_number), 
median)
  names(mydata.aggregate)[names(mydata.aggregate)=="Group.1"] <- "Xbin"
  names(mydata.aggregate)[names(mydata.aggregate)=="Group.2"] <- "Class_number"
  
  # Find number of cells of each type in each class
  a <- ddply(mydata,.(Metadata_Sample,Metadata_Scan,Xbin,Class_number),summarize,sum = 
length(ObjectNumber))
  b <- ddply(a,.(Xbin,Class_number),summarize,mean = mean(sum),sd = sd(sum))
  mydata.aggregate$Cell_count <- b[order(b[,2],b[,1]),]$mean
  
  # Finding factors
  factors <- which(sapply(mydata, is.factor))
  factors.ag <- which(sapply(mydata.aggregate, is.factor))
  
  ######################
  
  #Deselect non classifiable attributes
  select <- c("ImageNumber","ObjectNumber","Metadata_Experiment","Metadata_Image","X",
              
"Metadata_Sample","Metadata_Scan","Metadata_Time","Class_number","Xbin","Class_Number",
              
"AreaShape_Center_X","AreaShape_Center_Y","Location_Center_X","Location_Center_Y",
              "Globalposition_X","Pillar_Height","Cell_count")
  
  X.unselect <- mydata.aggregate
  X <- X.unselect[!colnames(X.unselect) %in% select]
  N <- length(X[,1]) # Number of observations
  classNumber <- X.unselect$Class_number
  
  mydata.aggregate.sd <- 
aggregate(mydata[,10:136],list(mydata$Xbin,mydata$Class_number), sd)
  
  
==PAGE:107==
  
  
  return(list(Xbin = mydata$Xbin, 
X=X,X.unselect=X.unselect,N=N,classNumber=classNumber,select=select,sd = 
mydata.aggregate.sd))
  
}
